About Me
Name: Ultra (originally Ultrawoman)
Gender: Female
Age: 35
Location: England

Latest Info (4th Nov 2019)
For anyone who may be concerned about my lack of Gilmore Girls fics right now, there will be more. I'm working on plans for The Literati Advent Calendar 2019 and then there will be other new stories in 2020 too. For Hart of Dixie, I'm working double-time on One Step At A Time right now, with a view to having it complete by the end of November, and Growing Up Kinsella Style will continue to be regularly updated until the end of the month, before it goes on hold until the new year. This year's Christmas one-shots will be on the theme of 'Christmas Miracle' and in the fandoms of Firefly, Timeless, Hart of Dixie, and Avengers! ;)
Ultra

Dislikes (A-Z)

Note - if you like my dislikes or dislike my likes, that is totally cool. I try not to judge people and don't expect to be judged by others. We all are who we are, and I believe we should be tolerant and non-judgemental, wherever possible :)
